    product_name VARCHAR(255),
    brand_id INT,
    category_id INT,
    FOREIGN KEY (brand_id) REFERENCES Brand(brand_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (category_id) REFERENCES Category(category_id)
);

    product_name VARCHAR(255),
    brand_id INT,
    category_id INT,
    FOREIGN KEY (brand_id) REFERENCES Brand(brand_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (category_id) REFERENCES Category(category_id)
);
